\DoxyCodeLine{00538\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ public\ domain\ branchless\ UTF-\/8\ decoder\ by\ Christopher\ Wellons:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00539\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ https://github.com/skeeto/branchless-\/utf8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00540\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Decode\ the\ next\ character,\ c,\ from\ s,\ reporting\ errors\ in\ e.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00541\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00542\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Since\ this\ is\ a\ branchless\ decoder,\ four\ bytes\ will\ be\ read\ from\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00543\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ buffer\ regardless\ of\ the\ actual\ length\ of\ the\ next\ character.\ This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00544\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ means\ the\ buffer\ \_must\_\ have\ at\ least\ three\ bytes\ of\ zero\ padding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00545\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ following\ the\ end\ of\ the\ data\ stream.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00546\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00547\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Errors\ are\ reported\ in\ e,\ which\ will\ be\ non-\/zero\ if\ the\ parsed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00548\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ character\ was\ somehow\ invalid:\ invalid\ byte\ sequence,\ non-\/canonical}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00549\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ encoding,\ or\ a\ surrogate\ half.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00550\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00551\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ function\ returns\ a\ pointer\ to\ the\ next\ character.\ When\ an\ error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00552\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ occurs,\ this\ pointer\ will\ be\ a\ guess\ that\ depends\ on\ the\ particular}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00553\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ error,\ but\ it\ will\ always\ advance\ at\ least\ one\ byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00554\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00555\ \mbox{\hyperlink{base_8h_a69201cb276383873487bf68b4ef8b4cd}{FMT\_CONSTEXPR}}\ \textcolor{keyword}{inline}\ \textcolor{keyword}{auto}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_a9cd935fa9e8ecf106e59bee1411440b9}{utf8\_decode}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*\ \mbox{\hyperlink{main-override_8cpp_a1384e7608274313a9433fa573868557b}{s}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{eabase_8h_a435d1572bf3f880d55459d9805097f62}{uint32\_t}}*\ c,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}*\ e)}
